# Bolt Food Metrics Glossary - Looker Hierarchy

This comprehensive knowledge base contains all unique metrics organized by Looker Explore and Group Labels. This structure helps you:

1. **Understand Metrics**: Find detailed descriptions for any metric mentioned in analysis
2. **Build Dashboards**: Identify which Looker Explore and metrics to use for specific business questions

## How to Use This Guide

- **For Understanding Metrics**: Use Ctrl+F to search for a specific metric name
- **For Dashboard Building**: Navigate by Looker Explore to see all available metrics grouped by business function
- **Metric Deduplication**: If a metric appears in multiple explores/groups, all locations are listed

---

## ⭐ Info - Basket Items

### Basket metrics - Item metrics

**Dishes per Order, :**

Average number of primary dish basket items (parentless, active items) per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Items per Order, :**

Average number of basket item records (including main dishes, modifiers, replacements, and compliments) per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Merchant Price After Discounts per Item, €**

Average provider price after discounts per delivered dish, expressed in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Merchant Price Before Discounts per Item, €**

Average provider price before discounts per delivered dish, expressed in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price After Discounts without VAT, $**

Total local-currency value of active basket items after discount excluding VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price After Discounts without VAT, €**

Total EUR value of active basket items after discount excluding VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price After Discounts, $**

Total local-currency value of active basket items after discount including VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price After Discounts, €**

Total EUR value of active basket items after discount including VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price Before Discounts without VAT, $**

Total local-currency value of active basket items before discount excluding VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price Before Discounts without VAT, €**

Total EUR value of active basket items before discount excluding VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price Before Discounts, $**

Total local-currency value of active basket items before discount including VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Total Item Price Before Discounts, €**

Total EUR value of active basket items before discount including VAT, aggregated per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Products → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Unique Items per Order, :**

Average count of distinct basket item identifiers per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

### Business review - Commissions & incentives total

**Item-Level Discount Promo Share, %**

Percentage of delivered provider price before discounts attributable to items with menu campaign discounts (campaign_id is not null) over the total delivered provider price per provider Product and hour.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

### Business review - GMV per order

**Merchant Price After Discounts per Order, €**

The average provider price after discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Merchant Price Before Discounts per Order, €**

The average provider price before discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

### Business review - GMV total

**Total Merchant Price After Discounts, €**

The total provider price after discounts in EUR for delivered orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Total Merchant Price Before Discounts without VAT, $**

The total provider price before discounts without vat for delivered orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Total Merchant Price Before Discounts without VAT, €**

The total provider price before discounts without vat in EUR for delivered orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Total Merchant Price Before Discounts, $**

The total provider price before discounts for delivered orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Total Merchant Price Before Discounts, €**

The total provider price before discounts in EUR for delivered orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---


## ⭐ Info - Couriers

### Courier growth - Active couriers

**New Active Courier Count, #**

The count of unique root couriers who completed their first delivery, based on their first delivered order timestamp.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier growth - Active couriers*

---

### Courier growth - Online couriers

**New Online Courier Count, #**

The count of unique root couriers who became active online for the first time, based on their first active timestamp.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier growth - Online couriers*

---


## ⭐ Info - Merchant Leads

### Provider Onboarding - Escalation

**Merchant Ops Escalation Rate, %**

Share of cases escalated to provider ops team

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider Onboarding - Escalation*

---

**Merchant Ops Escalation Resolution Time, Min**

Average resolution time for provider ops escalations (in minutes), per case

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider Onboarding - Escalation*

---

### Provider Onboarding - Onboarding SLA

**Lead Asset Delivery Within 72 Hrs Sla, %**

Share of providers delivering assets within 72 hours (≤ 4320 minutes)

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider Onboarding - Onboarding SLA*

---

**Lead Menu Creation Within 24 Hrs Sla, %**

Share of providers creating menu within 24 hours (≤ 1440 minutes)

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider Onboarding - Onboarding SLA*

---

**Lead Onboarded Within 5 Days, %**

Share of providers onboarding completion within 5 days

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider Onboarding - Onboarding SLA*

---

**Lead Onboarding Qualification Within 24 Hrs Sla, %**

Share of providers qualifying onboarding within 24 hours (≤ 1440 minutes)

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider Onboarding - Onboarding SLA*

---


## ⭐ Info - Merchants

### Provider growth - Merchant growth

**New Active Merchant Count, #**

The count of providers who became active for the first time.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider growth - Merchant growth, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Provider growth - Merchant growth*

---

Average number of primary dish basket items (parentless, active items) per delivered order.

Average number of basket item records (including main dishes, modifiers, replacements, and compliments) per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Basket Items → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

---

**Merchant Price After Discounts per Item, €**

Average provider price after discounts per delivered dish, expressed in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Basket Items → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Basket metrics - Item metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Basket metrics - Item metrics*

Average provider price before discounts per delivered dish, expressed in EUR.

---

### Business review - Bolt Plus

**Bolt Plus Agency Fee Share of Aov, %**

Average bolt plus agency fee amount per order as a percentage of Average Order Value (AOV).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Bolt Plus Agency Fee Share of Gmv, %**

Average bolt plus agency fee amount per order as a percentage of Gross Merchandise Value (GMV).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Bolt Plus Enrolled Provider GMV Share, %**

GMV for bolt plus enrolled providers as share of Total GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Bolt Plus GMV Share, %**

The share of GMV attributed to bolt plus deliveries within the total GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Bolt Plus User Order Frequency, :**

The quantity of delivered bolt plus orders divided by the quantity of distinct users who placed bolt plus orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Delivered Bolt Plus Orders Count, #**

The total count of delivered bolt plus orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**GMV Before Discounts per Bolt Plus Order, €**

The average gross merchandise value (GMV) before discounts in EUR per delivered bolt plus order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Merchant Price Before Discounts per Bolt Plus Order, €**

The average provider price before discounts in EUR per delivered bolt plus order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

**Total Bolt Plus GMV Before Discounts, €**

The total gross merchandise value (GMV) before discounts in EUR for delivered bolt plus orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Bolt Plus, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Bolt Plus*

---

### Business review - Commissions & incentives per order

**Merchant Commission Share of Aov, %**

Average commission amount per order as a percentage of Average Order Value (AOV).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order*

---

**Merchant Commission Share of Gmv, %**

Average commission amount per order as a percentage of Gross Merchandise Value (GMV).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order*

---

**Provider Demand Refund Deduction GMV Share, %**

The share of provider refund deduction (auto and manual) within the total GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order*

---

**Provider Demand Refund Deduction per Order, €**

The average amount deducted automatically from the provider in the case of a demand refund.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order*

---

**Refund Dispute Amount per Order, €**

The average amount paid back to the provider following a dispute regarding a demand refund deduction.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives per order*

---

### Business review - Commissions & incentives total

**GMV With Delivery Fee Campaign GMV Share, %**

The share of GMV attributed to deliveries with a delivery fee discount, within the total GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

**Platform Orders Merchant Commission, €**

Provider commission in EUR for delivered Platform orders (`delivery_type = 'platform'`).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

**ROD Orders Merchant Commission, €**

Provider commission in EUR for delivered own-delivery (ROD) orders (`delivery_type = 'own_delivery'`).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

**Takeaway Orders Merchant Commission, €**

Provider commission in EUR for delivered takeaway orders (`delivery_type = 'takeaway'`).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

**Total Merchant Commission, $**

Provider commission in local currency for delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

**Total Merchant Commission, €**

Provider commission in EUR for delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Commissions & incentives total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Commissions & incentives total*

---

### Business review - GMV contributions per vertical

**Delivery Food GMV Share, %**

The share of GMV attributed to food deliveries within the total GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV contributions per vertical*

---

**Delivery Store GMV Share, %**

The share of GMV attributed to store deliveries within the total GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV contributions per vertical*

---

### Business review - GMV per order

**Calculated Eater Surge per Order, $**

The average eater surge in local currency per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

The average eater surge in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Delivery Price After Discounts per Order, $**

The average delivery price after discounts in local currency per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Delivery Price After Discounts per Order, €**

The average delivery price after discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Delivery Price Before Discounts per Order, $**

The average delivery price before discounts in local currency per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Delivery Price Before Discounts per Order, €**

The average delivery price before discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Eater Fees GMV Share, %**

2. The average share of eater fee to GMV, calculated as ((service_fee_eur + small_order_fee_eur + delivery_price_before_discount_eur) / order_gmv_eur) per delivered order, then averaged across all delivered orders within the time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Eater Fees Revenue GMV Share, %**

The average share of delivery revenue  to GMV for all delivered orders excluding orders utilizing restaurant own delivery, then averaged across all delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Eater Fees per Order, €**

The average of eater fee in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period. The eater fee consists of (service_fee_eur + small_order_fee_eur + delivery_price_before_discount_eur).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**GMV After Discounts per Order, €**

The average gross merchandise value (GMV) after discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**GMV Before Discounts per Order, €**

The average gross merchandise value (GMV) before discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Merchant Price After Discounts per Order, $**

The average provider price after discounts in local currency per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Merchant Price After Discounts per Order, €**

The average provider price after discounts in EUR per delivered order within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Basket Items → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV per order*

---

**Merchant Price Before Discounts per Order, $**

The average provider price before discounts in local currency per delivered order within a specific time period.

### Business review - GMV total

**Eater Fees Revenue, €**

The revenue from delivery fee componenets collected from eaters(excluding orders utilising restaurant own deliveries and incomplete orders) to GMV.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**GMV Cash Orders Before Discounts, €**

The total gross merchandise value (GMV) before discounts in EUR where the payment method type was 'cash' for all delivered orders within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**GMV Platform Orders Before Discounts, €**

GMV before discounts for delivered Platform orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**GMV ROD Orders Before Discounts, €**

GMV before discounts for delivered own-delivery (ROD) orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**GMV Takeaway Orders Before Discounts, €**

GMV before discounts for delivered takeaway orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Not Responded Order Price After Discounts, €**

Total provider price after discounts for orders where the provider never responded.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Not Responded Order Price Before Discounts, $**

Total provider price before discounts for orders where the provider never responded.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Not Responded Order Price Before Discounts, €**

Total provider price before discounts for orders where the provider never responded.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Rejected Order Price After Discounts, €**

The total provider after before discounts for orders rejected by the provider within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Rejected Order Price Before Discounts, $**

Total provider price before discounts for orders that were rejected by the provider.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Rejected Order Price Before Discounts, €**

Total provider price before discounts for orders that were rejected by the provider.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - GMV total, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - GMV total*

---

**Total Calculated Eater Surge, $**

The total eater surge for delivered orders within a specific time period.

---

**Total Calculated Eater Surge, €**

The total eater surge in EUR for delivered orders within a specific time period.

The total delivery price after discounts for delivered orders within a specific time period.

**Total Delivery Price After Discounts, €**

The total delivery price after discounts in EUR for delivered orders within a specific time period.

**Total Delivery Price Before Discounts, €**

The total delivery price before discounts in EUR for delivered orders within a specific time period.

### Business review - Order count

**Courier Delivered Orders Count, #**

Total number of delivered orders based on order activation time.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Business review - Order count, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**Delivered Own Delivery Orders Count, #**

The total count of delivered orders for rod.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**Delivered Platform Orders Count, #**

Count of delivered orders that were fulfilled on the platform network (`delivery_type = 'platform'`).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**Delivered Takeaway Orders Count, #**

Count of delivered orders that were fulfilled as takeaway (`delivery_type = 'takeaway'`).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**Merchant Delivered Orders Count, #**

The total count of delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**Placed Orders Count, #**

The total count of orders placed within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**User Delivered Orders Count, #**

The total count of orders delivered to users.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**User Order Frequency, :**

The quantity of delivered orders divided by the quantity of distinct users who placed orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

**User Placed Orders Count, #**

The total count of orders placed by users within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

### Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order

**Courier Distance Base Earnings, €**

Average base distance earnings earned by couriers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Distance Multiplier Earnings, €**

Average distance earnings from proactive multipliers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Distance Proactive Multiplier Earnings, €**

Average courier earnings from distance-based proactive multipliers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Dropoff Base Earnings, €**

Average base dropoff earnings earned by couriers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Dropoff Multiplier Earnings, €**

Average dropoff earnings from proactive multipliers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Dropoff Proactive Multiplier Earnings, €**

Average courier earnings from dropoff proactive multipliers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

### Courier performance - Courier acceptance

**Courier Delivery Completion Rate, %**

Rate of deliveries that were both picked up and delivered by couriers.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Redispatch Accidental Acceptance Rate, %**

Share of orders redispatched because the courier accpeted by mistake out of all accepted orders. Accepting by mistake is labeled when time between acceptance and rejection is less or equal to 15 seconds.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Redispatch Courier Changes Mind Rate, %**

Share of orders redispatched because the courier accpeted and changed their mind out of all accepted orders. Accepting by mistake is labeled when time between acceptance and rejection is less or equal to 60 seconds.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Redispatch During Pickup Rate, %**

Share of orders redispatched before order has been picked up out of all accepted orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

---

### Courier performance - Courier distance per order

**Courier Dropoff Distance per Order, Km**

Average distance (in meters) traveled by the courier from the provider to the eater, per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

**Courier Dropoff Speed per Order, Km/h**

Average courier speed (in km/h) during the dropoff leg of the delivery (provider to eater), per delivered non-batched order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

**Courier Pickup Distance per Order, Km**

Average distance (in meters) traveled by the courier from their location to the provider, per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

**Courier Pickup Speed per Order, Km/h**

Average courier speed (in km/h) during the pickup leg of the delivery (courier to provider), per delivered non-batched order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

**Courier Total Distance per Order, Km**

Average total courier route distance per delivered order, in kilometers.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

### Courier performance - Courier time per order

**Courier Acceptance Duration, Min**

The average time (in minutes) couriers take to accept an order after it has been assigned.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Accepted to Picked Up Duration, Min**

Average courier accepted to picked up time in minutes.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier After Order Wait Time, Min**

The average time (in minutes) couriers spend waiting for the next order after dropping off.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Dropping Off Order, Min**

For all delivered orders the average duration between order marked as picked up and order marked as dropped off.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Picking Up Order, Min**

For all delivered orders the average duration between MAX(courier arrived at provider, order waiting for pickup) and order marked as picked up.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Pickup to Delivered, Min**

For delivered orders the average time in minutes between when the courier picks up the order and when the order is delivered.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Redispatch Duration, Min**

The average time (in minutes) spent on redispatching an order per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Time per Order, Min**

For delivered orders the average time delivery courier spent on delivering an order. Duration between accepting an order to marking it delivered.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Travelling to Merchant, Min**

For all delivered orders the average pickup travel duration.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Wait From Target Arrival, Min**

For all delivered orders the average time courier needs to wait at the provider in cases when they arrive before target arrival time. If food is marked ready before target arrival timestamp, food ready timestamp is used instead.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Wait Until Target Arrival, Min**

For all delivered orders the average time courier needs to wait at the provider to pick up the order compared to the target arrival time. If courier arrives after target arrival time, duration between arrival and order marked ready timestamps is used.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

### Delivery quality - CS ticket order

Share of orders that have a delivery quality tickets submitted by eater. Delivery quality tickets are about courier delivery actions (courier not moving, courier was rude, order damaged etc.).

---

**Timing Quality Ticket Rate, %**

Share of orders that have a timing related tickets submitted by eater. Timing tickets are about delays (order took longer, order was delayed, order arrived cold etc.).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - CS ticket order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - CS ticket order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - CS ticket order*

---

### Delivery quality - Late order

**Late Delivery Order -5 Min Rate, %**

Order delivered up to 5 min later than initial ETA upper bound value.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Delivery Order 10min+ Rate, %**

Share of orders delivered more than 10 min later than initial ETA upper band.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Delivery Order 5-10 Min Rate, %**

Order delivered 5-10 min later than initial ETA upper bound value.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Delivery Order Rate, %**

Share of orders delivered with a drop off delay. Drop off delay is defined as delivering order later than the initial ETA upper bound.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Courier Late Rate, %**

Share of orders picked up late due to courier being late. Pickup delay is defined as picking up the order at least 5 min later compared food marked ready for pickup timestamp.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Merchant Early Rate, %**

Share of orders picked up late due to providers preparing food faster than estimated. Pickup delay is defined as picking up the order at least 5 min later than food was marked ready for pickup.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Order 10-15 Min Rate, %**

The total count of delivered orders used to calculate the late pickup order 10-15 min rate.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Order 5-10 Min Rate, %**

The total count of delivered orders used to calculate the late pickup order 5-10 min rate.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Order Rate, %**

Share of orders picked up late. Pickup delay is defined as picking up the order at least 5 min later than food was marked ready for pickup.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

---

**Batched Order Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders by courier that were delivered as part of a batch.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Post-courier Assignment Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of a batch and batch creation happened after order assignment (instant batch algorithm).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Pre-courier Assignment Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of a batch and batch creation happened before order assignment (batch routing algorithm).

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Same Merchant Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of same-provider batch.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

### Orchestration - Order wait time

**Median Order Duration, Min**

The median delivered time, or p50, in minutes, for orders with a status of delivered.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Handover Duration, Min**

For all delivered orders the average handover duration from handover offer to handover closing, i.e. from MIN(courier arrived at provider, order waiting for pickup) until order marked as picked up.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Ready to Delivered, Min**

For delivered orders the average duration between order waiting for pickup and order delivered timestamps.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Total Wait Time, Min**

Average total order waiting for pickup minutes. Duration between order marked ready for pickup and order picked up timestamps.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Wait Until Target Arrival, Min**

Average order waiting for pickup time in cases where provider finished earlier. Either courier marked ready or target arrival time is used, depending which one happened earlier.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Total Order Duration, Min**

The average time (in minutes) from when an order is activated to when it is delivered, calculated only for orders with delivery_type = 'platform'.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

For all delivered orders average absolute error between estimated and actual pickup travel durations.

---

## ⭐ Info - Sessions

### Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed

**Merchant Viewed From Home Category Rate, %**

Proportion of sessions where a provider was viewed from the home category.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Merchant Viewed From Main Feed Rate, %**

Proportion of sessions where a provider was viewed from the main feed.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Merchant Viewed From Search Rate, %**

Proportion of sessions where a provider was viewed from search.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Merchant Viewed Rate, %**

Proportion of sessions where any provider was viewed.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Session Search Usage Rate, %**

Proportion of sessions where search was used.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Time to 1st Merchant Viewed per Session, Min**

Average minutes from session start to first provider viewed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed Before Product Added per Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed per session before first product added event.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed From Home Category per Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed from the home category per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed From Main Feed per Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed from the main feed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed From Search per Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed through search per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed per Converted Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed per converted session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed per Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Unique Merchants Viewed per Unconverted Session, :**

Average number of distinct providers viewed per unconverted session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

**Zero Available Providers Instance Search Rate, %**

The proportion of search sessions with at least one instance of zero available results shown in search.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session funnel - 1. Merchant viewed*

---

### Session metrics - Selection

**Estimated Orders Lost From Eater Surge, #**

Estimated number of lost orders due to eater surge pricing (price multiplier applied to delivery fees).

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Estimated Orders Lost From Pause Demand Incentives, #**

Estimated number of lost orders due to demand campaigns pausing.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Estimated Orders Lost From Radius Shrinkage, #**

Estimated number of lost orders due to radius shrinkage (temporary reduction in the delivery radius).

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Food Merchant Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of food providers displayed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Food Merchant Within 4km Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of food providers displayed per session within 4 km distance.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Merchant Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of providers displayed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Merchant Within 4km Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of providers displayed per session within 4 km distance.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Store Merchant Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of store providers displayed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Store Merchant Within 4km Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of store providers displayed per session within 4 km distance.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Busy Ratio, :**

The ratio of active orders to the number of online couriers in a session, calculated within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Courier Earnings Dynamic Multiplier, :**

Average dynamic multiplier applied to courier earnings per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Delivery Fee Dynamic Multiplier, :**

Average dynamic multiplier applied to the delivery fee per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Per-Merchant Closure, %**

The ratio of providers closed due per-provider closing mechanism to the total provider count in a session, calculated within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Radius Shrinkage, %**

The ratio of providers closed due to radius shrinkage to the total provider count in a session, calculated within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Selection*

---

### Session metrics - Sessions count

**Menu Food Views, #**

The distinct count of sessions that viewed a food provider's menu, within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session metrics - Sessions count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Sessions count*

---

**Menu Store Views, #**

The distinct count of sessions that viewed a store provider's menu, within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session metrics - Sessions count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Sessions count*

---

**Menu Views, #**

The distinct count of sessions that viewed a provider's menu, within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Users → Session metrics - Sessions count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Session metrics - Sessions count*

---

**Sessions All Users Count, #**

The total count of sessions started within a specific time period.

## ⭐ Info - Store documents

### Store - 1P Financials - COGS

**Total COGS Item Count, #**

Total count of items sold. This metric represents the number of units sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount with VAT, $**

Total COGS in local currency before supplier discount, including VAT and bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount with VAT, €**

Total COGS in EUR before supplier discount, including VAT and bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount without VAT, $**

Total COGS in local currency before supplier discount, excluding VAT and including bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount without VAT, €**

Total COGS in EUR before supplier discount, excluding VAT and including bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item with VAT, $**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in local currency, including VAT and bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item with VAT, €**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in EUR, including VAT and bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item without VAT, $**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in local currency, excluding VAT but including bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item without VAT, €**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in EUR, excluding VAT but including bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

### Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments

**Total Inventory adjustment Live Count item Count, #**

Total count of inventory adjustment items due to live. This metric represents the number of units adjusted due to live, aggregated by movement creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. It is calculated by summing up the units of all document items where document_subtype = 'live' AND document_type = 'inventory'.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments*

---

**Total Inventory adjustment Live item, $**

Total value of inventory adjustment items due to live in local currency, excluding VAT. This metric represents the financial impact of live adjustments for store operations in the store's local currency. It is calculated by summing up the value of all document items where document_subtype = 'live' AND document_type = 'inventory', without VAT included, and converted to the local currency.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments*

---

**Total Inventory adjustment Live item, €**

It is calculated by summing up the value of all document items where document_subtype = 'live' AND document_type = 'inventory', without VAT included.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - Inventory Adjustments*

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs*

---

**Total Writeoff Item W3 Discounted expiry, $**

Total value of writeoff items due to discounted expiry in local currency, excluding VAT. This metric represents the financial impact of waste due to discounted expiry for store operations in the store's local currency. It is calculated by summing up the value of all document items where document_subtype_category = 'W3 | Discounted expiry (waste)', without VAT included, and converted to the local currency.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs*

---

**Total Writeoff Item W3 Discounted expiry, €**

Total value of writeoff items due to discounted expiry in EUR, excluding VAT. This metric represents the financial impact of waste due to discounted expiry for store operations in EUR currency. It is calculated by summing up the value of all document items where document_subtype_category = 'W3 | Discounted expiry (waste)', without VAT included.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs*

---

It is calculated by summing up the units of all document items where document_subtype_category = 'W4 | Other internal losses (waste)'.

## ⭐ Metrics - Couriers

### Business review - Order count

**Courier Delivered Orders Count, #**

Total number of delivered orders based on order activation time.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Business review - Order count, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Business review - Order count, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Business review - Order count*

---

### Courier activity - Courier lifecycle

**Hard Churn Courier Count, #**

The total count of hard churn events at the hard churn timestamp (after at least 31 consecutive days of inactivity), where each event corresponds to a unique root courier that can hard churn only once within a single month.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier activity - Courier lifecycle*

---

**Permanent Churn Courier Count, #**

The total count of permanent churn events at the permanent churn timestamp (after at least 90 consecutive days of inactivity), where each event corresponds to a unique root courier who can permanently churn only once within a single month.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier activity - Courier lifecycle*

---

**Resurrected Courier Count, #**

The total count of resurrection events at the resurrection timestamp (after returning to activity following hard churn, i.e. at least 31 consecutive days of inactivity), where each event corresponds to a unique root courier who can be resurrected only once within a single month.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier activity - Courier lifecycle*

---

**Soft Churn Courier Count, #**

The total count of soft churn events at the soft churn timestamp (after at least 14 consecutive days of inactivity), where multiple events can come from the same root courier within a single month.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier activity - Courier lifecycle*

---

### Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per hour

**Courier cost per online hour, €**

Courier cost including adjustment divided by courier online hours.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per hour*

---

**Courier cost per utilised hour, €**

Courier cost including adjustment divided by courier utilised hours.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per hour*

---

---

**Courier Total Earnings, €**

Average total earnings paid to couriers per delivered order, in EUR. Includes base, multiplier, top-up, and wait compensation earnings.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Total Multiplier Earnings, €**

Average total earnings from proactive and reactive (dynamic) multipliers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Total Pickup Earnings, €**

Average pickup earnings earned by couriers per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier Wait Time Compensation, €**

Average compensation paid for courier wait time at provider per delivered order, in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Courier cost per order, €**

Courier cost per order including adjustment.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Effective Multiplier Rates Distance, :**

Average distance-based effective multiplier rate per delivered order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

---

**Effective Multiplier Rates Dropoff, :**

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier delivery costs per order*

### Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics

**Total Invoiced Courier Bonus, $**

Total invoiced courier bonus in local currency.

**Total Invoiced Courier Bonus, €**

Total invoiced courier bonus in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics*

---

**Total Invoiced Courier Cash Paid to Merchant with Adjustments, €**

Total adjusted cash transaction when courier was paid by the eater during a cash order. Lowers partner’s balance (i.e., the cash amount is actually bigger than initially processed).

---

**Total Invoiced Courier Cash Received From Eater with Adjustments, €**

Total adjusted cash transaction when courier was paid by the eater during a cash order. Increases partner’s balance (i.e., the cash amount is actually smaller than initially processed).

---

**Total Invoiced Courier Costs, $**

Total of courier earnings, courier bonus, courier deduction, courier waiting at provider compensation, and courier adjustments in local currency.

---

**Total Invoiced Courier Costs, €**

Total of courier earnings, courier bonus, courier deduction, courier waiting at provider compensation, and courier adjustments.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics*

**Total Invoiced Courier Deductions, $**

Total invoiced courier adjustments in EUR.

---

**Total Invoiced Courier Earnings, $**

Total invoiced courier earning without adjustments in local currency.

Total invoiced courier earning without adjustments in EUR.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier costs - Courier invoice metrics*

**Total Invoiced Courier Tips, $**

### Courier performance - Courier acceptance

**Courier Acceptance Rate, %**

Share of orders accepted by couriers out of all order proposals.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Courier Delivery Completion Rate, %**

Rate of deliveries that were both picked up and delivered by couriers.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Courier Did Not Respond Rate, %**

Share of orders where couriers did not respond out of all order proposals.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Courier Proposed Orders Count, #**

Total number of orders proposed to the courier.

---

**Courier Redispatch Duration, Min**

Courier time for orders accepted but not delivered due to courier redispatching the order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Redispatch Rate, %**

Share of orders accepted but not delivered due to courier redispatching the order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Courier Redispatch by CS Rate, %**

Share of orders accepted but not delivered due to courier redispatching the order through the CS.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Courier Redispatch in App Rate, %**

Share of orders accepted but not delivered due to courier redispatching the order through the courier app.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Courier Rejection Rate, %**

Share of orders rejected by couriers out of all order proposals.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Redispatch Accidental Acceptance Rate, %**

Share of orders redispatched because the courier accpeted by mistake out of all accepted orders. Accepting by mistake is labeled when time between acceptance and rejection is less or equal to 15 seconds.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Redispatch Courier Changes Mind Rate, %**

Share of orders redispatched because the courier accpeted and changed their mind out of all accepted orders. Accepting by mistake is labeled when time between acceptance and rejection is less or equal to 60 seconds.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

**Redispatch During Pickup Rate, %**

Share of orders redispatched before order has been picked up out of all accepted orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier acceptance, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier acceptance*

---

Average courier speed (in km/h) during the dropoff leg of the delivery (provider to eater), per delivered non-batched order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier distance per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier distance per order*

---

### Courier performance - Courier time per order

**Courier Acceptance Duration, Min**

The average time (in minutes) couriers take to accept an order after it has been assigned.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Accepted to Picked Up Duration, Min**

Average courier accepted to picked up time in minutes.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier After Order Wait Time, Min**

The average time (in minutes) couriers spend waiting for the next order after dropping off.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Dropping Off Order, Min**

For all delivered orders the average duration between order marked as picked up and order marked as dropped off.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Picking Up Order, Min**

For all delivered orders the average duration between MAX(courier arrived at provider, order waiting for pickup) and order marked as picked up.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Pickup to Delivered, Min**

For delivered orders the average time in minutes between when the courier picks up the order and when the order is delivered.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Time per Order, Min**

For delivered orders the average time delivery courier spent on delivering an order. Duration between accepting an order to marking it delivered.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Travelling to Merchant, Min**

For all delivered orders the average pickup travel duration.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Wait From Target Arrival, Min**

For all delivered orders the average time courier needs to wait at the provider in cases when they arrive before target arrival time. If food is marked ready before target arrival timestamp, food ready timestamp is used instead.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

**Courier Wait Until Target Arrival, Min**

For all delivered orders the average time courier needs to wait at the provider to pick up the order compared to the target arrival time. If courier arrives after target arrival time, duration between arrival and order marked ready timestamps is used.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Courier performance - Courier time per order, ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier time per order*

---

### Courier performance - Courier utilisation

**Courier Deliveries per Hour, :**

Average number of deliveries completed per hour by couriers.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier utilisation*

---

**Courier Total Online Hours, :**

Hours courier was online in the courier app. Sum of hours spent on delivering orders and waiting for orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier utilisation*

---

**Courier Total Utilised Hours, :**

Hours courier was online in the courier app and spent on delivering orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier utilisation*

---

**Courier Utilisation Rate, %**

Percentage of online hours spent delivering orders, calculated as utilised hours divided by total online hours.

*Also available in: ⭐ The Delivery Explore → Courier performance - Courier utilisation*

---
