### Delivery quality - Late order

**Late Delivery Order -5 Min Rate, %**

Order delivered up to 5 min later than initial ETA upper bound value.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Delivery Order 10min+ Rate, %**

Share of orders delivered more than 10 min later than initial ETA upper band.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Delivery Order 5-10 Min Rate, %**

Order delivered 5-10 min later than initial ETA upper bound value.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Delivery Order Rate, %**

Share of orders delivered with a drop off delay. Drop off delay is defined as delivering order later than the initial ETA upper bound.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Courier Late Rate, %**

Share of orders picked up late due to courier being late. Pickup delay is defined as picking up the order at least 5 min later compared food marked ready for pickup timestamp.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Merchant Early Rate, %**

Share of orders picked up late due to providers preparing food faster than estimated. Pickup delay is defined as picking up the order at least 5 min later than food was marked ready for pickup.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Order 10-15 Min Rate, %**

The total count of delivered orders used to calculate the late pickup order 10-15 min rate.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Order 5-10 Min Rate, %**

The total count of delivered orders used to calculate the late pickup order 5-10 min rate.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

**Late Pickup Order Rate, %**

Share of orders picked up late. Pickup delay is defined as picking up the order at least 5 min later than food was marked ready for pickup.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Late order, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Late order*

---

### Delivery quality - Order rating

**Bad Courier Rating Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders with a bad courier rating by eater (1-3 star rating).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Bad Merchant Rating Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders with a bad provider rating by eater (1-3 star rating).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Bad Order Provider Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders with a bad provider rating by eater (1-3 star rating) OR Missing/Wrong Item Ticket OR Refunded Amount > 0.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Bad Rating Order Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders with either bad courier or provider rating by eater (1-3 star rating).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Good Courier Rating Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders with a positive courier rating by eater.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Good Merchant Rating Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders with a good provider rating by eater (4-5 star rating).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Merchant Rating per Order, :**

Average rating given to providers by eaters, excluding orders with missing ratings.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

**Missing Courier Rating Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that do not have a courier rating value.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Delivery quality - Order rating, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Delivery quality - Order rating*

---

### Orchestration - Batched orders

**Batched Multi-Merchant Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of multi-provider batch.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Order Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders by courier that were delivered as part of a batch.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Users → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Post-courier Assignment Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of a batch and batch creation happened after order assignment (instant batch algorithm).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Pre-courier Assignment Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of a batch and batch creation happened before order assignment (batch routing algorithm).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

**Batched Same Merchant Rate, %**

Share of delivered orders that were delivered as part of same-provider batch.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Batched orders, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Batched orders*

---

### Orchestration - Order wait time

**Median Order Duration, Min**

The median delivered time, or p50, in minutes, for orders with a status of delivered.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Handover Duration, Min**

For all delivered orders the average handover duration from handover offer to handover closing, i.e. from MIN(courier arrived at provider, order waiting for pickup) until order marked as picked up.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Ready to Delivered, Min**

For delivered orders the average duration between order waiting for pickup and order delivered timestamps.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Total Wait Time, Min**

Average total order waiting for pickup minutes. Duration between order marked ready for pickup and order picked up timestamps.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Order Wait Until Target Arrival, Min**

Average order waiting for pickup time in cases where provider finished earlier. Either courier marked ready or target arrival time is used, depending which one happened earlier.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

**Total Order Duration, Min**

The average time (in minutes) from when an order is activated to when it is delivered, calculated only for orders with delivery_type = 'platform'.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Orchestration - Order wait time, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Orchestration - Order wait time*

---

### Provider Onboarding - Salesforce Leads

**Leads Active Bistro Count, #**

Number of leads active on Bistro (Slovakian delivery platform).

---

**Leads Active Bolt Count, #**

Count of leads that are currently active on the Bolt platform.

---

**Leads Active Bolt Only Count, #**

Count of leads active exclusively on Bolt.

---

**Leads Active Bolt and Competitor Count, #**

Count of leads that are active both on Bolt and on at least one competitor platform.

---

**Leads Active Bolt and Primary Competitor Count, #**

Number of leads active on both Bolt and with Primary comeptitor platforms in that zone.

---

**Leads Active Competitors Count, #**

Count of leads active on any competitor platform.

---

**Leads Active Competitors Only Count, #**

Count of leads active only on competitor platforms (not Bolt).

---

**Leads Active Delivery Platforms Count, #**

Total number of delivery platforms where a lead is active (can include multiple platforms).

---

**Leads Active Foodora Count, #**

Number of leads active on the Foodora platform.

---

**Leads Active Foody Count, #**

Number of leads active on the Foody platform.

---

**Leads Active Glovo Count, #**

Number of leads active on the Glovo platform.

---

**Leads Active Primary Competitor Count, #**

Number of leads active on the primary competitor platform.

---

**Leads Active Pyszne Count, #**

Number of leads active on Pyszne (Polish delivery platform).

---

**Leads Active Takeaway Count, #**

Number of leads active on the Takeaway platform.

---

**Leads Active Tazz Count, #**

Number of leads active on Tazz (Romanian delivery platform).

---

**Leads Active UberEats Count, #**

Number of leads active on Uber Eats.

---

**Leads Active Wolt Count, #**

Number of leads active on the Wolt platform.

---

**Leads Count, #**

Total number of provider leads within the zone and vertical.

---

**Leads Coverage Rate, :**

It indicates the ratio of all total identified leads onboarded to Salesforce that are actively engaged on the Bolt platform.

---

**Leads Overlap Rate, :**

It represents the share of leads that are active on both Bolt and at least one competitor platform at the same time.

---

**Leads Primary Competitor Overlap Rate, :**

It represents the proportion of leads that are simultaneously active on both Bolt and the primary competitor’s platform within a given zone at a same time.

---

**Leads Top Brands Count, #**

Total number of top-tier brand provider leads within the zone and vertical.

---

### Provider activity - Merchant availability

**Merchant Available Sessions, #**

Sessions for which the provider was available.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant availability*

---

**Merchant PPC Closed Count, #**

The total count of unique providers who were closed due to PPC during the specified time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant availability*

---

**Merchant SKU Sessions Availability Rate, %**

The session-weighted availability rate for a provider SKU, calculated as the average availability (1.0 when available, 0.0 when not available) across all hourly measurements, weighted by the number of times the provider was viewed in sessions during each hour. It does only include active, selleable items.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant availability, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Provider activity - Merchant availability*

---

### Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle

**Delivered Orders per Merchant, :**

The distinct count of delivered orders per providers with 1+ delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

**ELC Active Merchant Count, #**

The total count of unique providers (merchants) who were active for at least one second during the specified time period and were still within their early lifecycle phase.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

The total count of delivered orders placed with providers that were in the ELC period at the time of order creation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

Total Number of Churned Providers.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

Total Number of Resurrected Providers.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

**PoP Merchant Churn Count, #**

The count of providers who were active in one period but became inactive in the next period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

**PoP Merchant Churn Rate, %**

The percentage of active providers in one period who became inactive in the next period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

---

**PoP Merchant Resurrected Count, #**

The count of providers who were inactive in one period but became active again in the next period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Provider activity - Merchant lifecycle*

### Session metrics - Selection

**Estimated Orders Lost From Eater Surge, #**

Estimated number of lost orders due to eater surge pricing (price multiplier applied to delivery fees).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Estimated Orders Lost From Pause Demand Incentives, #**

Estimated number of lost orders due to demand campaigns pausing.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Estimated Orders Lost From Radius Shrinkage, #**

Estimated number of lost orders due to radius shrinkage (temporary reduction in the delivery radius).

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Median Food Merchant Count Shown per Session, :**

Median number of food providers displayed per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

Median number of food providers displayed per session within 4 km distance.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

Median number of providers displayed per session.

---

Median number of store providers displayed per session within 4 km distance.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Busy Ratio, :**

The ratio of active orders to the number of online couriers in a session, calculated within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Courier Earnings Dynamic Multiplier, :**

Average dynamic multiplier applied to courier earnings per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

Average dynamic multiplier applied to the delivery fee per session.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Per-Merchant Closure, %**

The ratio of providers closed due per-provider closing mechanism to the total provider count in a session, calculated within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

---

**Session Weighted Radius Shrinkage, %**

The ratio of providers closed due to radius shrinkage to the total provider count in a session, calculated within a specific time period.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Sessions → Session metrics - Selection*

### Store - 1P Financials - COGS

**Total COGS Item Count, #**

Total count of items sold. This metric represents the number of units sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount with VAT, $**

Total COGS in local currency before supplier discount, including VAT and bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount with VAT, €**

Total COGS in EUR before supplier discount, including VAT and bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount without VAT, $**

Total COGS in local currency before supplier discount, excluding VAT and including bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item before supplier discount without VAT, €**

Total COGS in EUR before supplier discount, excluding VAT and including bottle deposits, for orders. Computed only for documents where document_type = 'order'. -  - Business context - - Suppliers may issue temporary discounts via dedicated promo pricelists layered on base lists. - - This metric uses undiscounted baseline prices to evaluate negotiation effectiveness relative to promo terms. - - Intended for KPI/analytical purposes; not a financial accounting metric.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item with VAT, $**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in local currency, including VAT and bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item with VAT, €**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in EUR, including VAT and bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

**Total COGS Item without VAT, $**

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in local currency, excluding VAT but including bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

---

Total Cost of Goods Sold (COGS) in EUR, excluding VAT but including bottle deposits, for order fulfillment operations. This metric represents the purchasing cost of items sold through orders, aggregated by order creation timestamp for reconciliation purposes. Only includes documents where document_type = 'order'. Bottle deposit values are included in the calculation.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - COGS, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - COGS*

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Store documents → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs, ⭐ Metrics - Products → Store - 1P Financials - Writeoffs*

---

It is calculated by summing up the value of all document items where document_subtype_category = 'S2 | Sold to 3rd party (waste)', without VAT included.

### Timing - Courier ETA

**Courier Arrival Time vs Merchant Eta, Min**

The average difference (in minutes) between courier target arrival time and provider ETA for delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

**Dropoff ETA Avg Absolute Error, Min**

The average mean absolute error (in minutes) of courier ETA predictions for dropoff.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

**Dropoff ETA Avg Error, Min**

The average mean error (in minutes) of courier ETA predictions for dropoff.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

**Dropoff ETA Missing Rate, %**

The average rate of missing courier ETA dropoff predictions for delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

**Pickup ETA Avg Absolute Error, Min**

For all delivered orders average absolute error between estimated and actual pickup travel durations.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

**Pickup ETA Avg Error, Min**

For all delivered orders average error between esimated and actual pickup travel durations.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Couriers → Timing - Courier ETA, ⭐ Metrics - Merchants → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

**Pickup ETA Missing Rate, %**

The average rate of missing courier ETA pickup predictions for delivered orders.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → Timing - Courier ETA*

---

---

### User growth - Bolt Plus

**Active Users Bolt Plus Count, #**

The total count of users with atleast one delivered bolt plus order.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Orders → User growth - Bolt Plus*

---

**Bolt Plus Churned Count**

The count of users with a gap of at least 90 days between their previous Bolt Plus subscription end date and either their next subscription start date (if they resubscribed) or the current date (if they haven’t).

---

**Bolt Plus First Subscriptions Count**

The count of users subscribing to bolt plus for the first time based on bolt plus first subscription date.

*Also available in: ⭐ Info - Users → User growth - Bolt Plus*

---

**Bolt Plus Renewed Subscriptions Count**

The count of users who subscribed to Bolt Plus at least one day after their previous Bolt Plus subscription end date, based on the subscription date.

---

**Bolt Plus Subscriptions Count**

The count of users subscribing to bolt plus based on bolt plus subscription date.

---

---

### User growth - User retention

**Delivery Core User 30day City Retention Rate, %**

Users who were activated more than 90 days ago in delivery within a specific city and made at least one transaction in the same city within 30 days after their last order.

---

**Delivery Core User 30day Zonal Retention Rate, %**

Users who were activated more than 90 days ago in delivery within a specific zone and made at least one transaction in the same zone within 30 days after their last order.

---

**Delivery New User 5wk Retention Rate, %**

New users who were activated in delivery less than 90 days ago and made at least one transaction during the fifth week following their activation date.

---

**Stores 1p Core User 30day City Retention Rate, %**

Users who were activated more than 90 days ago in Stores 1P within a specific city and made at least one Stores 1P transaction in the same city within 30 days after their last order.

---

**Stores 1p Core User 30day Zonal Retention Rate, %**

Users who were activated more than 90 days ago in Stores 1P within a specific zone and made at least one Stores 1P transaction in the same zone within 30 days after their last order.

---

**Stores 1p New User 5wk Retention Rate, %**

New users who were activated in Stores 1P less than 90 days ago and made at least one transaction in Stores 1P during the fifth week following their activation date.

---



---
